adjusted revenues* $16.5B, +18% organically*</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.33pt">Profit margin (GAAP) of 1.7%, +330 bps&#59; adjusted profit margin* 9.8%, +760 bps organically*</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.33pt">Continuing EPS (GAAP) of $0.08, +$0.36&#59; adjusted EPS* $0.82, +$0.99</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.33pt">Cash from Operating Activities (GAAP) of $1.9B, +$1.1B&#59; free cash flow* $1.7B, +$1.0B</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt"><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">BOSTON &#8212; October&#160;24, 2023 &#8212; GE (NYSE&#58;GE) announced results today for the third quarter ending September 30, 2023. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GE Chairman and CEO and GE Aerospace CEO H. Lawrence Culp, Jr. said, &#34;GE delivered another quarter of very strong results with double-digit growth in revenue, profit, and cash. At GE Aerospace, we continue to experience rapid growth driven by robust demand and solid execution, largely in Commercial Engines and Services. At GE Vernova, our Grid and now Onshore Wind businesses were both profitable this quarter and we expect their performance to continue to improve. With our two largest Renewable Energy businesses delivering and Power's continued strength, we remain highly confident in GE Vernova's spin-off next year.&#34;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Culp concluded, &#34;Based on our year-to-date results and continued momentum in the fourth quarter, GE is raising full-year 2023 guidance. We're well-positioned to launch GE Aerospace and GE Vernova as independent companies in the beginning of the second quarter. I'm more excited than ever about our path ahead.&#34; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GE Aerospace and GE Vernova continued to take recent action on their priorities&#58;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:1.75pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">GE Aerospace</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2.5pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.33pt">Delivered double-digit growth in orders, revenue, and operating profit driven by commercial momentum and strength in services. Orders grew 34% and revenue was up 25%, led by Commercial Engines and Services with Defense revenue up 8%, led by services and Edison Works.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2.5pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt;text-decoration:underline">Announced</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> the U.S Army&#8217;s acceptance of the first two GE Aerospace T901 flight test engines that will power the Future Attack Reconnaissance Aircraft prototypes. The T901 will also upgrade the U.S. Army's Apache and Black Hawk helicopters, providing 50% more power, reduced lifecycle costs, and lower fuel consumption.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2.5pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.33pt">Named executive leadership team members, including Tara DiJulio as Chief Corporate Affairs Officer, Christian Meisner as Chief Human Resources Officer, Jake Phillips as General Counsel, and Rob Giglietti as Treasurer. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:1.75pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:1.75pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">GE Vernova</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:6.82pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.67pt;vertical-align:baseline">1</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2.5pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.33pt">Drove strong revenue and operating profit growth in Renewable Energy and Power. Renewable Energy revenue grew 14% organically* with double-digit equipment growth in Grid, North America Onshore Wind, and Offshore Wind. Power also grew with revenue up 9% organically*. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2.5pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.33pt;text-decoration:underline">Accumulated</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> more than two million commercial operating hours for the advanced H-Class, heavy-duty gas turbine fleet, supporting HA services billings growing to $1 billion by mid-2020s&#59; this fleet now has an installed capacity of over 47 gigawatts globally, the equivalent of powering over 35 million U.S. homes. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2.5pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.33pt">Named Ken Parks as CFO, and Vic Abate to an expanded role as CEO of GE Vernova's Wind businesses.</font></div><div style="height:36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">* Non-GAAP Financial Measure</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">1 </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">GE's portfolio of energy businesses </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">1</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:36pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:6pt;padding-right:-6.75pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Total Company Results</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:3pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:95%">We present both GAAP and non-GAAP financial measures to provide investors with additional information.
